\f1\'b7\f0  What is Exploratory Testing?\par
\b  What is traceability matrix?\par
\b0 A tracebility matrix is a document that details the technical requirements for a given test scenario and its current state. It helps the testing team understand the level of testing that is done for a given product\par
A software process should help you keeping the virtual table up-to-date.\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is Boundary value testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is Equivalence partitioning testing?\par
\b  What is Integration testing?\par
\b0 Integration testing is a level of the software testing process where individual units are combined and tested as agroup.\par
Integration testing is done by a specific integration tester or test team.\par
There are 2 levels of integration testing:\par
\b 1)\b0 Component integration testing.\par
\b 2)\b0 System integration testing.\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What determines the level of risk?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is Alpha testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is beta testing?\par
 \b What is component testing?\b0\par
A minimal software item that can be tested in isolation. It means "A unit is the smallest testable part of software.\par
Unit testing is known as a component testing, module testing, program testing.\par
In unit testing white box testing method will apply.\par
 \b What is functional system testing?\b0\par
A requirement that specifies a function that a system component must perform.\par
functional testing involves black box testing.\par
There are two types of test approach: \par
1. Requirement based  functional testing\par
2. Process based testing\par
 \b What is Non-Functional Testing?\par
\b0 Non-Functional Testing the attributes of a component or system that do not relate ti functionality, e.g. reliability, efficiency, usability, interoperability, maintainability and portability.\par
It is the testing of "how" the system works. Non-Functional testing may be performed at all test levels.\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is GUI Testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is Adhoc testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is load testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is stress Testing?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is white box testing and list the types of white box testing?\par
\b  What is black box testing? What are the different black box testing techniques?\par
\b0 Testing, either functional or non-functional, without reference to the internal structure of the component or system.\par
The technique of testing without having any knowledge of the interior workings of the application is black box testing.\par

\f1\'b7\f0  What is 7 key principles? Explain in detail?\par
 \b Difference between QA v/s QC v/s Tester\par
\b0 QA (quality assurance), QC (quality control), and tester are related but distinct concepts in software development.\par
\b QA(Quality Assurance):\par

\pard{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}{\*\pn\pnlvlblt\pnf2\pnindent0{\pntxtb\'B7}}\fi-360\li720\sa200\sl276\slmult1\b0 Focues on processes and procedures rather than conducting actual testing on the system.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab} Process oriented activities.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}preventive activities.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}It is a subset of Software Test Life Cycle (STLC).\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1\par
\b QC(Quality Control)\par

\pard{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}{\*\pn\pnlvlblt\pnf2\pnindent0{\pntxtb\'B7}}\fi-360\li720\sa200\sl276\slmult1\b0 Focuses on actual testing by executing software with intend to identify bug/defect through implementation of procedures and process.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}product oriented activities.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}It is a corrective process.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}QC can be considered as the subset of Quality Assurance.\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1\par
\b Tester\par

\pard{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}{\*\pn\pnlvlblt\pnf2\pnindent0{\pntxtb\'B7}}\fi-360\li720\sa200\sl276\slmult1\b0 Focues on actual testing.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}Product oriented activities.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}It is a preventive process.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}Testing is the subset of Quality Control.\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1\par
In summary QA, QC and Testers work together to ensure software quality, with distinct responibilities and focus areas.\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1\f1\'b7\f0  Difference between Smoke and Sanity?\par
\f1\'b7\f0  Difference between verification and Validation\par
\f1\'b7\f0  Explain types of Performance testing.\par
\b  What is Error, Defect, Bug and failure?\par
\b0 A mistake in coding is called Error, Error found by tester is called Defect, defect accepted by development team then it is called bug, build does not meet the requirements then it is called failure.\par
\f1\'b7\f0  Difference between Priority and Severity\par
\f1\'b7\f0  What is Bug Life Cycle?\par
 \b Explain the difference between Functional testing and NonFunctional testing\par
\b0 Functional testing and Non-Functional testing are two distinct approaches to sofware testing:\par
Functional Testing:\par

\pard{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}{\*\pn\pnlvlblt\pnf2\pnindent0{\pntxtb\'B7}}\fi-360\li720\sa200\sl276\slmult1 Functional testing is performed using the functional specification provided by the client and verifies the system against the functional requirements.\b\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}\b0 Functional testing is executed first\b\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}\b0 Manual testing or automation tools can be used for functional testing\b\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}\b0 Business requirements are the inputs to functional testing\b\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}\b0 Easy to do manual testing\b\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1\b0  Non-Functional Testing:\par

\pard{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}{\*\pn\pnlvlblt\pnf2\pnindent0{\pntxtb\'B7}}\fi-360\li720\sa200\sl276\slmult1 Non-Functional testing checks the performance, reliability, scalability and other non-functional aspects of the software system.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}Non-Functional testing should be performed after functional testing.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}Using tools will be effective for this testing\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}performance parameters like speed, scalability are inputs to non-functional testing.\par
{\pntext\f2\'B7\tab}tough to do manual testing.\par

\pard\sa200\sl276\slmult1        To illistrate the difference: \par
       Functional Testing: Does the login button work correctly?\par
       Non-Functional Testing: How long does it take to log in? or can the                \tab software handle 1000 concurrent users? \par
  In summary, functional testing checks what the software does, while non-functional testing checks how well it doe it.\par
